## Idea

Transpositions are permutations that swap two elements.

## Definitions

### Transpositions

<pre class="Agda"><a id="5427" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="5434" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#5434" class="Module">_</a>

### Any transposition on a type equipped with a counting is a standard transposition

      <a id="19907" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19908" href="foundation-core.decidable-propositions.html#872" class="Function">type-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="19928" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19929" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="19933" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#12862" class="Bound">Y</a> <a id="19935" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#19872" class="Bound">x</a><a id="19936" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19939" class="Symbol">→</a>

        <a id="23919" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23920" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#6218" class="Function">has-decidable-equality-count</a> <a id="23949" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#12845" class="Bound">eX</a> <a id="23952" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23953" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="23957" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23958" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="23962" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#13276" class="Function">two-elements-transposition</a><a id="23988" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="23991" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#23764" class="Bound">x</a><a id="23992" class="Symbol">)</a>

        <a id="24079" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24080" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#6218" class="Function">has-decidable-equality-count</a> <a id="24109" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#12845" class="Bound">eX</a> <a id="24112" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24113" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="24117" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24118" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="24122" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#13276" class="Function">two-elements-transposition</a><a id="24148" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="24151" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#23766" class="Bound">y</a><a id="24152" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Transpositions can be transported along equivalences

          <a id="29927" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29929" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="29939" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="29941" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24283" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="29943" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="29946" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8459" class="Function">transposition</a> <a id="29960" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29726" class="Bound">t</a><a id="29961" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29963" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="29966" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#5721" class="Function">inv-equiv</a> <a id="29976" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24283" class="Bound">e</a><a id="29977" class="Symbol">))</a>
          <a id="29990" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29992" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29167" class="Function">correct-transposition-conjugation-equiv-list</a> <a id="30037" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29728" class="Bound">li</a> <a id="30040" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29732" class="Bound">x</a><a id="30041" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="30044" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
          <a id="30056" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30058" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a>
            <a id="30073" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30075" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="30077" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30077" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="30079" class="Symbol">→</a>
              <a id="30095" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a>
                <a id="30121" class="Symbol">((((</a><a id="30125" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24283" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="30127" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="30130" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#8459" class="Function">transposition</a> <a id="30144" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29726" class="Bound">t</a><a id="30145" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30147" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="30150" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30077" class="Bound">g</a><a id="30151" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30153" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="30156" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#11020" class="Function">permutation-list-transpositions</a> <a id="30188" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29728" class="Bound">li</a><a id="30190" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30192" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7869" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="30195" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#5721" class="Function">inv-equiv</a> <a id="30205" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24283" class="Bound">e</a><a id="30206" class="Symbol">)</a>
                <a id="30224" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30226" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#29732" class="Bound">x</a><a id="30227" class="Symbol">))</a>
            <a id="30242" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30244" href="foundation.equivalences.html#15838" class="Function">left-inverse-law-equiv</a> <a id="30267" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#24283" class="Bound">e</a><a id="30268" class="Symbol">)))</a>
</pre>
### For all `n : ℕ`, for each transposition of `Fin n`, there exists a matching transposition in `Fin (succ-ℕ n)`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="Fin-succ-Fin-transposition"></a><a id="30401" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30401" class="Function">Fin-succ-Fin-transposition</a> <a id="30428" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30430" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30431" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30431" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="30433" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30435" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1548" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="30436" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30438" class="Symbol">→</a>

    <a id="30487" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="30489" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="30491" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30491" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="30493" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30495" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4910" class="Function">has-cardinality</a> <a id="30511" class="Number">2</a> <a id="30513" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30514" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#515" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="30516" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30517" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2392" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="30521" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30431" class="Bound">n</a><a id="30522" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30524" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="30527" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30527" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="30529" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30531" href="foundation-core.decidable-propositions.html#872" class="Function">type-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="30551" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30552" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30491" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="30554" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#30527" class="Bound">x</a><a id="30555" class="Symbol">)))))</a> <a id="30561" class="Symbol">→</a>

        <a id="30641" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4910" class="Function">has-cardinality</a> <a id="30657" class="Number">2</a>
